
========== CONFIG ==========
R1: CARE HOME STAFFING SYSTEM v3.0 |  |  | 
R2: SELF-ORGANIZING EDITION |  |  | 
R4: SETTING | VALUE | UNIT | NOTES
R5: Roster Start Date | 2025-01-06 |  | Must be a Monday
R6: Cycle Length | 14 | days | Panama rotation period
R8: SHIFT TIMES & HOURS |  |  | 
R9: Early Shift (E) | 6 | hours | 08:00-14:00
R10: Late Shift (L) | 6 | hours | 14:00-20:00
R11: Full Day (EL) | 12.25 | hours | 07:45-20:00 (incl 15min handover)
R12: Night Shift (N) | 12.25 | hours | 19:45-08:00 (incl 15min handover)
R14: HANDOVER & BREAKS |  |  | 
R15: Evening Handover | 15 | mins | 19:45-20:00 (Day→Night overlap)
R16: Morning Handover | 15 | mins | 07:45-08:00 (Night→Day overlap)
R17: Break Deduction | 0 | hours | Breaks are PAID (care home requirement)
R19: MINIMUM STAFFING |  |  | 
R20: Early Min (Heads) | 3 | people | Minimum on Early
R21: Early Min (Skill) | 2 | points | Senior=1.0, Junior=0.5
R22: Late Min (Heads) | 3 | people | Minimum on Late
R23: Late Min (Skill) | 2 | points | Senior=1.0, Junior=0.5
R24: Night Min (Heads) | 3 | people | Minimum on Night
R25: Night Min (Skill) | 1.5 | points | At least 1 Senior
R27: OVERTIME & AGENCY |  |  | 
R28: OT Premium | 2 | £/hour | Extra for OC/OT shifts
R29: Agency Rate (Day) | 22 | £/hour | External day cover
R30: Agency Rate (Night) | 28 | £/hour | External night cover (12hr)
R32: SAFETY LIMITS |  |  | 
R33: Max Consecutive Days | 5 | days | Fatigue limit
R34: Max AL Same Day | 2 | people | Coverage protection
R35: Float Retainer | 50 | £/week | Standby payment
R37: ANNUAL LEAVE |  |  | 
R38: AL Entitlement | 28 | days/year | Standard UK
R40: WEEKLY HOURS TARGETS |  |  | 
R41: FT Target (EL workers) | 42.875 | hours/week | 3.5 shifts × 12.25hrs
R42: FT Target (E or L only) | 36 | hours/week | 6 shifts avg
R43: Night FT Target | 42.875 | hours/week | 3.5 shifts × 12.25hrs
R45: BANK HOLIDAY |  |  | 
R46: BH Premium | 1.5 | multiplier | Applied to base rate on bank holidays
R48: SICKNESS ASSUMPTIONS |  |  | 
R49: Avg Sickness Rate | 0.06 | % | 6% sector average (5-8% typical)
R50: Avg AL per day | 1 | people | Typical daily AL overlap
R51: AGENCY NIGHT SPLIT |  |  | 
R52: Night Gap % (of total) | 0.3 | 30% of gaps are night shifts | 
R54: FORTIFICATION PARAMETERS |  |  | 
R55: Night Float Priority | Y |  | 
R56: Emergency Call-In Premium | 1.5 |  | 
R57: Manager Floor Rate | 18 |  | 
R58: Winter Sick Uplift | 1.8 |  |

R4: Day of Week | [F:CHOOSE(MOD(B3-1,7)+1,"Mon","Tue","Wed","Thu","Fri","Sat","Sun")=Mon] |  |  |  |  |

========== AGENCY_KILL_GUIDE ==========
R1: THE "AGENCY KILLER" PROTOCOL |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R3: SHIFT TIMES (with 15-min Paid Handover) |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R4: Day Shift: 07:45-20:00 (12.25 paid hours) |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R5: Night Shift: 19:45-08:00 (12.25 paid hours) |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R6: Morning Handover: 07:45-08:00 (15 mins overlap) |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R7: Evening Handover: 19:45-20:00 (15 mins overlap) |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R8: Breaks: PAID (no deduction) |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R10: CORE CONCEPT |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R11: The Panama 2-2-3 rotation creates natural "short weeks" for each team. |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R12: During a short week, staff work only 2 days (24.5 hours) instead of 5 days (61.25 hours). |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R13: These staff are RESTED and UNDER-HOURS. They are your Agency Kill targets. |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R15: THE PATTERN (14-day cycle) |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R16:  | Mon | Tue | Wed | Thu | Fri | Sat | Sun
R17: Week 1 - Day A | ON | ON | off | off | ON | ON | ON
R18: Week 1 - Day B | off | off | ON | ON | off | off | off
R19: Week 2 - Day A | off | off | ON | ON | off | off | off
R20: Week 2 - Day B | ON | ON | off | off | ON | ON | ON
R21: (Night teams follow same pattern) |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R23: WEEKLY HOURS BREAKDOWN |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R24: Long Week (5 days × 12.25hrs): 61.25 hours |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R25: Short Week (2 days × 12.25hrs): 24.5 hours |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R26: Average per week: 42.875 hours (full-time) |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R28: AGENCY KILL TARGETS |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R29: Week 1: Day B staff are on short week (only Wed-Thu) → Target them for gaps Mon/Tue/Fri-Sun |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R30: Week 2: Day A staff are on short week (only Wed-Thu) → Target them for gaps Mon/Tue/Fri-Sun |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R32: GOLD SQUARES IN ROSTER |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R33: Any "OFF" cell highlighted in GOLD = This person is: |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R34:   • On their short week (rested) |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R35:   • Under their normal hours (hungry for money) |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R36:   • Your FIRST call before agency |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R38: THE WORKFLOW |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R39: 1. Gap appears (sickness, AL, etc) |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R40: 2. Look at ROSTER for that day |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R41: 3. Find GOLD squares = These are your targets |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R42: 4. Call them: "Want a shift? +£2/hr bonus" |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R43: 5. If they accept: Change their cell from OFF to OC-EL (On-Call Full Day) |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R44: 6. The cost tracker updates automatically |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R46: THE ECONOMICS (12.25-hour shifts) |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R47: Agency Day shift: £22/hr × 12.25 = £269.50 |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R48: Internal OT shift: £12.50/hr × 12.25 + £2 × 12.25 = £177.63 |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R49: SAVINGS PER SHIFT: £91.87 |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R51: Agency Night shift: £28/hr × 12.25 = £343 |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R52: Internal OT Night: £13/hr × 12.25 + £2 × 12.25 = £183.75 |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R53: SAVINGS PER NIGHT: £159.25 |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R55: FLOAT POOL RULES |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R56: Your 3 Float staff show as "AVL" (Available) every day. |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R57: Use them BEFORE calling overtime: |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R58:   • Change AVL → EL for day floor coverage |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R59:   • Change AVL → ADM for admin/paperwork |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R60:   • Change AVL → TRN for training |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R61: Floats get base hours, not OT premium (they are scheduled, not called in). |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R63: FATIGUE PROTECTION |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R64: Do NOT assign OT to anyone who has worked 5+ consecutive days. |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R65: Check the FATIGUE_TRACKER tab before assigning overtime. |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R66: Purple = BLOCK from further OT until they rest. |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R68: HANDOVER PROTOCOL |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R69: 07:45: Day staff arrive, Night staff brief them (15 mins) |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R70: 08:00: Night staff leave, Day staff take over |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R71: 19:45: Night staff arrive, Day staff brief them (15 mins) |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R72: 20:00: Day staff leave, Night staff take over |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
R73: Both teams are PAID for the 15-min handover overlap. |  |  |  |  |  |  |
